## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="06575-1805">Atributos de Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="06575-1805">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="06575-1806">Esta clase contiene los siguientes atributos para Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="06575-1806">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
